The most common cause is a Gradle limitation: the plugins applied to subprojects should be consistent.
Please try the following:
1. Apply the Dokka and Kotlin plugins to the root project using the `plugins {}` DSL.

The most common cause is a Gradle limitation: the plugins applied to subprojects should be consistent.
Please try the following:
1. Apply the Dokka and Kotlin plugins to the root project using the `plugins {}` DSL.

The most common cause is a Gradle limitation: the plugins applied to subprojects should be consistent.
Please try the following:
1. Apply the Dokka and Kotlin plugins to the root project using the `plugins {}` DSL.

Please try the following:
1. Apply the Dokka and Kotlin plugins to the root project using the `plugins {}` DSL.

warning: Dokka could not load KotlinBasePlugin in project ':wgsl:cli', even though plugin org.jetbrains.kotlin.multiplatform is applied.
The most common cause is a Gradle limitation: the plugins applied to subprojects should be consistent.
Please try the following:
1. Apply the Dokka and Kotlin plugins to the root project using the `plugins {}` DSL.
   (If the root project does not need the plugins, use 'apply false')
2. Remove the Dokka and Kotlin plugins versions in the subprojects.
For more information see:
 - https://docs.gradle.org/current/userguide/plugins_intermediate.html#sec:plugins_apply
 - https://github.com/gradle/gradle/issues/25616
 - https://github.com/gradle/gradle/issues/35117
Please report any feedback or problems https://kotl.in/dokka-issues

kotlin scripting plugin: created the scripting discovery configuration: kotlinScriptDef
kotlin scripting plugin: created the scripting discovery configuration: testKotlinScriptDef

warning: Dokka could not load KotlinBasePlugin in project ':wgsl:core', even though plugin org.jetbrains.kotlin.multiplatform is applied.
The most common cause is a Gradle limitation: the plugins applied to subprojects should be consistent.
Please try the following:
1. Apply the Dokka and Kotlin plugins to the root project using the `plugins {}` DSL.
   (If the root project does not need the plugins, use 'apply false')
2. Remove the Dokka and Kotlin plugins versions in the subprojects.
For more information see:
 - https://docs.gradle.org/current/userguide/plugins_intermediate.html#sec:plugins_apply

 - https://github.com/gradle/gradle/issues/35117

warning: Dokka could not load KotlinBasePlugin in project ':wgsl:glsl', even though plugin org.jetbrains.kotlin.multiplatform is applied.
The most common cause is a Gradle limitation: the plugins applied to subprojects should be consistent.
Please try the following:
1. Apply the Dokka and Kotlin plugins to the root project using the `plugins {}` DSL.
   (If the root project does not need the plugins, use 'apply false')
2. Remove the Dokka and Kotlin plugins versions in the subprojects.
For more information see:
 - https://docs.gradle.org/current/userguide/plugins_intermediate.html#sec:plugins_apply
 - https://github.com/gradle/gradle/issues/25616
 - https://github.com/gradle/gradle/issues/35117

warning: Dokka could not load KotlinBasePlugin in project ':wgsl:hlsl', even though plugin org.jetbrains.kotlin.multiplatform is applied.
The most common cause is a Gradle limitation: the plugins applied to subprojects should be consistent.
Please try the following:
1. Apply the Dokka and Kotlin plugins to the root project using the `plugins {}` DSL.
   (If the root project does not need the plugins, use 'apply false')
2. Remove the Dokka and Kotlin plugins versions in the subprojects.
For more information see:
 - https://docs.gradle.org/current/userguide/plugins_intermediate.html#sec:plugins_apply
 - https://github.com/gradle/gradle/issues/25616
 - https://github.com/gradle/gradle/issues/35117

warning: Dokka could not load KotlinBasePlugin in project ':wgsl:msl', even though plugin org.jetbrains.kotlin.multiplatform is applied.
The most common cause is a Gradle limitation: the plugins applied to subprojects should be consistent.
Please try the following:
1. Apply the Dokka and Kotlin plugins to the root project using the `plugins {}` DSL.
   (If the root project does not need the plugins, use 'apply false')
2. Remove the Dokka and Kotlin plugins versions in the subprojects.
For more information see:
 - https://docs.gradle.org/current/userguide/plugins_intermediate.html#sec:plugins_apply
 - https://github.com/gradle/gradle/issues/25616
 - https://github.com/gradle/gradle/issues/35117
